The `public contributions` and `private contributions` by users in Malawi on `2022/11/17 1:13 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Malawi` and cities `Lilongwe` `Blantyre` `Mzuzu` `Zomba` `Karonga`.

There are `138 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/gayanvoice/top-github-users).

There are `900 users`  in Malawi. You need at least `0 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.

- GitHub Action - [gayanvoice/top-github-users-action](https://github.com/gayanvoice/top-github-users-action)
